Ma Shexiang's Telegram Clarifying the Gansu Incident - Most Urgent To the Central Party Headquarters, Party Headquarters of all provinces and cities, all Yuan and Ministry Councils, Chairmen of all provincial governments, Deputy Commander Zhang of Beiping, Commanders-in-Chief of all routes, Commanders, Division and Brigade Commanders, all legal entities, and all newspapers: I recently submitted a telegram to Chairman Chiang of the National Government, stating: Regarding the Gansu Incident, I previously presented it to the government and the Yuan based on telegrams from various parties. I recently saw a telegram from all sectors of Gansu party, government, military, agriculture, commerce, and academia, stating: Provincial Chairman Ma Hongbin was detained, Lei Zhongtian was publicly elected as Commander-in-Chief of the Gansu Security Forces, and Ma Wenche was concurrently appointed as Chairman, and has already taken office. I also submitted a telegram to Your Excellency on the [day name omitted] day, which I trust you have clearly noted. The telegram listed Hongbin's usurpation of political power and protection of bandits, and falsely accused Fu Xiang and Hongbin of the military disasters in Liangzhou and Zhenfan. Those who know the political situation in Gansu can immediately refute its falsity, and it is not worth refuting. However, I still cannot refrain from saying a word to Your Excellency: Hongbin was appointed as acting chairman of Gansu Province in December of last year, at a time when Gansu was in the aftermath of a great war, bandits were rampant, refugees were everywhere, the province had no government, and the people were in dire straits. Hongbin, as a native of the province, accepted the mandate at a time of chaos and struggled to cope, feeling overwhelmed. Therefore, he repeatedly pleaded for the appointment of a more capable person to avoid mediocrity. After two months, compelled by repeated telegrams from the central government and the continuous calls from all sectors of the province, he had no choice but to travel lightly from Ningxia to Lanzhou. At the same time, he also declared to Your Excellency that he would temporarily act for a maximum of two months. After arriving in the province, he mediated disputes, settled refugees, and showed great care for the troops stationed in Lanzhou, and repeatedly telegraphed to protect Cai and other members dispatched by the central government, including Ma Wenche, demonstrating harmony and mutual assistance. All these facts are documented and cannot be distorted by Fu Xiang alone. As for the reorganization of the Gansu provincial government, it was because all members of the Gansu province, except for the chairman, had not been appointed for half a year, and they shirked their responsibilities when things happened, making it impossible to deal with them. The central government, mindful of the importance of border administration, appointed members from the old members and inspectors to specialize in responsibility. Although Hongbin still served as chairman, he repeatedly telegraphed his resignation after receiving the order, stating that he was temporarily serving in a transitional capacity, which shows that he has always been indifferent to fame and fortune, and this should be known to Your Excellency. The telegram falsely accused him of seizing political power, which is contrary to the facts. As for Fu Xiang personally, he has been away from the province for more than ten years, and although he has respect for his homeland, he is deeply wary of his nephews. When Commander Gu Zhutong was ordered to enter Gansu, Fu Xiang repeatedly telegraphed to urge him and repeatedly begged Your Excellency to urge him to proceed quickly, as he feared that the conspiracy would last for a long time and hidden dangers would arise. It would be fortunate for Hongbin to be relieved of his responsibilities as soon as possible. The telegram also arbitrarily fabricated and falsely accused Xiang personally, which is laughable. As for the fact that Gansu has suffered from military disasters for many years, which are blamed on Xiang and others, this is even further from the truth. Zhenfan and Liangzhou have suffered from military banditry, which occurred in the 17th and 18th years of the Republic of China, while Hongbin had already led troops from Ningxia to the east in the 16th year, and Fu Xiang had also been away from Gansu for a long time. He only heard about the disasters in his hometown. Moreover, Fu Xiang's entire family suffered the most from the banditry in those years, and the houses in Dahe and Ningxia were burned down. The facts are all there, so who should be blamed? As for Ma Tingxian and others, they are not of the same clan as Xiang, and their intentions are incompatible. Last winter, when Hongbin was ordered to govern Gansu, Ma Tingxian immediately opposed him, and the documents are all there and can be reviewed. How can they be confused? Hongbin has been deferential in everything since becoming acting chairman. The guards of the provincial government and various cities are all stationed by Lei Zhongtian's troops. He has never brought a single soldier when entering and leaving the office. Since he has been entrusted with his life and family, how can he be said to have entered the city in plain clothes? All these inverted and obscured words are not worth the sneer of a knowledgeable person. As for whether the various sections mentioned in the telegram are factual, if public morality has not been completely extinguished, it is not difficult to distinguish right from wrong. At present, a small number of troops near Lanzhou have all been withdrawn, and the troops stationed in Ningxia, Suiliang, and Qinghai are also guarding their original defenses, and are all subject to the fair handling of the central government. However, I am mindful that Gansu has suffered from military drought for a long time, and all sectors of the province are supporting the central government and praying for peace. Now, there is such an unreasonable telegram. If it is not coercion, it must be a fabricated name. The manipulation is only by one or two people. Your Excellency's virtue and power are far-reaching. I implore you to distinguish right from wrong, rectify discipline, pacify the west, and secure the borders. The country is fortunate, Gansu is fortunate. I await your instructions in fear and trembling. Fu Xiang is old and has been away from his hometown for more than ten years. He has always had the intention of retiring, but he has been falsely accused for no reason. He is ashamed of his lack of virtue and unable to help the difficulties of the time. However, there are constant penalties in the country for abandoning discipline and inverting right and wrong. I fear that rumors from afar will confuse the facts, so I have sent this communication. I hope you will understand. Ma Fuxiang bows on the [day name omitted] day.

Yingshang Telegram to Shen Bao Newspaper: The Yingshang flood and bandit disasters have been reported in the Dongyang and [name omitted] telegrams. However, the severity and horror of the bandit disaster still needs to be described in detail. In addition to looting property along the Huai River, the bandits also took away more than 500 hostages and more than 300 sailboats. The hostages and boatmen were all killed without exception. Their methods of killing were extremely cruel, including cutting off arms, cutting off legs, burning with fire, or drowning in water. The various atrocities are heartbreaking to describe. In total, the number of people who died at the hands of the bandits is no less than 2,000, on par with those who died in the flood. The grass and trees smell of blood, and the rivers flow with crimson. The bodies floating on the water are all incomplete. The sailboats move freely up and down, and no one has escaped danger. They fled in panic and were in a state of utter disarray. They had no food and no shelter, and fathers, sons, brothers, husbands, and wives cried bitterly and lost each other. How can they survive the rest of their lives? I respectfully submit this third telegram and earnestly request your newspaper to widely appeal for relief. Yingshang Red Swastika Society bows respectfully.

Gaoyou Telegram to Shanghai Shen Bao Newspaper: Greetings. Recently sent a telegram to the Chinese and Foreign Relief Association and the Jiangsu Relief Association, stating: Heaven has sent disaster, and floods are rampant. Gaoyou is the convergence point of the Huai, Yi, Mu, and Si rivers. The terrain is low-lying. Since the summer, it has been raining continuously for days, and the rivers and lakes are roaring. The 11th and 12th districts west of the lake have become a swamp first. After the opening of the three seawalls, the water rushed and the embankments collapsed. The 1st to 10th districts were completely submerged. The autumn harvest has not been reaped, and not a single grain has been collected. People and animals have died, and houses have been washed away. The rooftops and tree tops are crowded with disaster victims, barely rescued. The miserable situation of 10,000 mouths crying for starvation is imminent. I implore your association to show great compassion and immediately allocate funds and send personnel to distribute emergency relief to save those who are about to die. On behalf of the 600,000 disaster victims, I bow nine times and beg you. I respectfully submit this telegram on your behalf and earnestly request that it be published in your newspaper to widely appeal for help. The survivors left after the disaster are grateful for your kindness and virtue. County Magistrate Wang Long of Gaoyou respectfully bows and seals.

Harbin Telegram to all newspapers: Since the beginning of autumn, continuous rain has fallen in the southern provinces of China, and mountain floods have erupted. The Jiang, Huai, Xiang, and Han rivers have successively breached their banks, causing widespread flooding. According to newspaper reports, the flooded area covers sixteen provinces and regions, and more than 30 million people are awaiting relief. The loss of life and property is countless. All four major issues of people's livelihood, namely clothing, food, housing, and transportation, are completely trapped in a desperate situation. The dead cannot be brought back to life, and the living can only wait for death. The mainland is about to sink, and its fish are sighing. The tragic situation is truly unbearable to see and unbearable to hear. People from all walks of life in Harbin, with the mentality of being hungry for the hungry and drowning for the drowning, are taking collective action. On the 29th of this month, a joint conference was convened to discuss relief matters. The Harbin Flood Relief Association of all provinces was organized and announced on the same day. Chief Executive Zhang Jinghui was publicly elected as the president of the association, and executive committee members and standing committee members were appointed to establish general affairs, fundraising, accounting, propaganda, and liaison departments to specialize in their respective duties. The association headquarters is located upstairs in the office of the Chief Executive of Nangan in this city, and began operating on the same day, raising funds and transporting grain as much as possible. Once a certain amount has been collected, it will be reported to the Central Relief Committee for distribution to the disaster areas. Although it is a drop in the bucket, it is a sincere effort to share the disaster and alleviate the suffering. The date of establishment of this association and the situation of the relief efforts are hereby reported to you by telegram. I implore you to pay attention. Harbin Flood Relief Association of all provinces bows respectfully. Dihua Jin Shuren Telegram to all newspapers: It has long been obvious to all and heard by all that the communist bandit Ma Zhongying has brought disaster to Gansu. In the summer of this year, he again used the name of the Commander-in-Chief of the Gansu-Ningxia-Qinghai Allied Army to occupy the Liangzhou area of Gansu, hired foreign rogues, gathered red bandits, established a pseudo-government, and created a state of terror. He was repeatedly defeated by the Gansu army. In early July, while our defense forces were advancing to suppress the rebellious Tanguts, he led thousands of bandits to attack and occupy Zhenxi County, forcing the good people to join the gang, colluding with the rebellious Tanguts to become bandits, looting and ravaging the area. The cattle, horses, and property of the people were all branded and taken away. His cruel acts were no different from those of the communist bandits. Because of the difficult transportation in Xinjiang and the defense forces being stationed on the border, it was difficult to gather them for a while. The bandit then besieged the Hami Mining Bureau, and hundreds of miles were poisoned. Countless Tanguts died tragically. By late July, our army concentrated and advanced in separate directions. In the battles of Liaojiawan and Suzhoufang, Ma Zhongjie, the younger brother of the bandit Ma Zhongying, was killed, and hundreds of bandits were killed. In the battle outside Zhenxi City, the younger brother of Ma Heiying, the bandit's pseudo-city defense commander, was killed by our artillery. The pseudo-city defense commander was also seriously injured. The remnants of the bandits retreated to the Tianshan Temple. Zhenxi County was recovered on August 6. The rebellious Tanguts, seeing the bandit's greed and love of killing and seeing the bravery of our army, surrendered one after another. They have been granted amnesty and allowed to rehabilitate themselves, and strong men have been selected to join our army to jointly attack the bandits. I have also strictly ordered the generals of all routes to track down and suppress the bandits. They have won every battle and captured many. The bandit leader Ma Zhongying is in a desperate situation and has retreated to Qincheng, northeast of Hami, carrying greasy goods. A siege plan has been drawn up, and the extermination is imminent. It is Shuren's duty to not let the bandits harm the people and cause trouble for the government in the west and the people to be ravaged. This telegram is sent to relieve your concerns. Chairman of Xinjiang Provincial Government and Border Defense Supervisor of Xinjiang Jin Shuren bows.

Important News

Central and National Government Memorial Week 56

Zhu Jiaju reports on the reorganization of university education

Yu Youren reports on the national disaster within the national disaster

Ma Fuxiang reports on the Gansu coup

At 9:00 AM on August 31, the Central Party Headquarters held a memorial week in the Great Auditorium. Central Committee members Ding Weifen, Zhu Jiaju, Ding Chaowu, Fang Juehui, Yu Jingtang, Miao Peicheng, Kexing'e, Wang Boling, and others, as well as officials from various departments and guests, about 500-600 people, attended. After Chairman Ding Weifen performed the ceremony, Zhu Jiaju reported that the Party has been working hard on China's education in recent days, even in the midst of hardship and difficulty. Even in terms of national education funding, especially higher education, it has increased significantly compared to the past. However, the results of education are not developing and progressing in proportion to the increase in funding. At present, many university graduates in our country have no way out, and specialized careers feel a lack of talent, which cannot be said to be a failure of university education. The general performance of this higher examination was not good, which is a reflection of the poor performance of university education. In my opinion, to build a new country, we must first cultivate the talents needed. We must formulate a weekly, appropriate, comprehensive, and precise plan for higher education. The politics of Soviet Russia are not worth discussing, but its education plan cannot be ignored. Its current plan, which ends in the autumn of 1933, requires 440,000 engineers and middle-level engineering personnel. Among the engineers working in the Moscow industry, there are 5,264 engineers and 6,175 middle-level engineering personnel. By October 1931, Moscow alone would need 13,879 engineers and 24,882 middle-level engineering personnel. After the completion of the five-year plan, 90,000 higher specialists and 360,000 middle-level talents are needed in agriculture. Agricultural manufacturing plants require 12,000 engineers and middle-level engineering personnel. The forestry sector requires 11,600 higher specialists and 27,000 middle-level specialists. The transportation sector requires 30,000 engineers and 120,000 middle-level engineering personnel. In addition, 65,000 doctors need to be trained. In terms of normal education, efforts are being made to create 80,000 primary school teachers. The education of other countries also has excellent plans. Looking back at our country, we talk about refreshing politics, promoting industry, and striving for various constructions every day, but we have not paid special attention to the talents needed, and we have not made accurate budgets. Some people advocate starting with construction first, and waiting for construction to succeed, education will naturally develop, which is a one-sided view. If we want to do construction without seeking universal education, and without accurate budgets and preparations for higher education, it is impossible. Moreover, the current university graduates are not the talents that the country truly needs, so social stability will also be affected. The so-called construction is just empty talk. For the current plan, we must reorganize university education: (1) There is no need to take the vanity of a large scale, open more departments, set up more courses, and hire more faculty and staff to expand expenses. The most important thing is the equipment of various books and instruments, so that students can get a good foundation, arouse academic interest, and guide them to work independently. On the one hand, we must provide professors with opportunities to study advanced academic knowledge and enhance the culture of the country and society. (2) Various departments should be connected and pay attention to basic subjects. In general, university students prefer new and different subjects, and those who run schools often cater to the students' ideas. Those who study philosophy do not value an introduction to philosophy and the history of philosophy, but pay attention to Kant's Critique of Pure Reason. The Department of Economics does not value an introduction to economics, but pays attention to Marx's Das Kapital. In the Department of Geology, there must be a specialized lecturer in paleontology. In the physics aspect, there must be Einstein's theory of relativity. As a result of this phenomenon, we only understand bits and pieces of advanced knowledge, but we do not understand basic and common problems, so how can we make further progress? We who run universities and educators in the country should be responsible for correcting this. (3) We must cancel duplicate courses and carefully allocate lectures to avoid putting the cart before the horse and building one house on top of another. We must also find ways to provide professors and students with frequent opportunities to make contact, so that students can have the convenience of asking and correcting questions in academic aspects, so as to arouse research interest, and also obtain considerable benefits in the cultivation of personality. (4) Strictly hold graduation examinations to avoid students with inferior grades from taking qualifications as a stepping stone for future advancement, so as not to mislead the country and society. If China wants to improve the status of university graduates, and count the talents of China, and check the results of university education, there must be a very carefully held university graduation examination, etc. After the report, the meeting adjourned at 10:00.

On the same morning, the National Government held the Premier's Memorial Week. Officials from various Yuan and Ministry Councils Yu Youren, Zhu Peide, Niu Yongjian, Ma Fuxiang, He Yaozu, Ru Yuli, Li Shuhua, and others, and more than 200 staff members attended. Chairman Yu Youren reported on the national disaster within the national disaster, saying that he still reports on the flood today, with infinite heartache. The water level of the rivers has not decreased in recent days, and Jiangbei has repeatedly warned of danger. The people are drifting away and separating. Governments of various countries have sent telegrams of condolence, and people from various countries have started raising donations. We can only express our gratitude for this. Regarding disaster relief, there is now a Flood Relief Committee dedicated to taking responsibility. I hope that the disaster relief colleagues can very quickly help the victims. The government issued an order to all officials in the country a few days ago, and ordered the Supervisory Yuan to send personnel to various flood prevention and disaster areas to investigate political achievements. In this serious national disaster, we want to see whether the officials and those responsible for water management and flood prevention have fulfilled their duties. I put forward a slogan here, that is, senior officials go to the people. The government's decision to donate salaries to help disaster relief is to make all officials show concern for the people in times of trouble. We must not only donate our salaries, but also donate our entire heart to the disaster victims. This significance is really important. Because of this flood, I thought of the great earthquake in Japan a few years ago. After the earthquake in Japan, the government and the people, united as one, quickly made up for their losses and restored their original state. We should strive in hardship and enable our country and nation to regain happiness from hardship. This is the responsibility that the whole country should bear together. After Yu finished reporting, Ma Fuxiang temporarily requested to report on the Gansu coup. He said that the Gansu coup was sudden, and the traffic was inconvenient, and the rumors were untrue. I have talked to the press about the truth of this matter many times, but it is not detailed. I would like to talk to you about it here. (The general idea is the same as Ma's [day name omitted] telegram) He also said that Ma Hongbin is not a remnant of Feng Yuxiang. Ma Hongbin was not in Gansu at the time of the changes in the 18th year. This time, he served as the chairman of Gansu entirely to serve his hometown, not to fight for political power. The central government has its own balance on this matter, and I do not want to say more now. However, I hope that you will uphold the late Premier's legacy of equality among all ethnic groups in the country, and advocate fairness in this matter, and do not cause greater disputes by being moved by the saying of Han-Hui ethnic struggle. Finally, he also reported in detail on his work experience in recent years. After the report, the meeting adjourned.

The Terrible Water Disaster in Sichuan 57

Countless Homes and Fields Submerged

Hundreds of Thousands of Victims

Chongqing Dispatch: Since the beginning of summer this year, Sichuan province has been plagued by incessant rain, causing mountain torrents and a sharp rise in the water levels of various rivers. Riverside counties have become virtually submerged, devastating farmland and collapsing houses. This has left impoverished residents and small merchants along the riverbanks without shelter or means of livelihood. Cries for relief are heard daily. A summary of the disaster situation in various areas is as follows:

Chengdu: Heavy rain began on August 1st and continued until the next day. Low-lying areas outside the city were quickly flooded. In the Upper and Middle Lotus Pond areas of the South Gate, the water was over two feet deep. The South Gate tunnel had water reaching above the knees. Fields and roads near the Outer South Dragon King Temple to the Youth Palace were all submerged. Inside the city, the water level in the streets and alleys was also above the knees. On the 3rd, torrential rain resumed, lasting for several days. The streets inside the city were once again transformed into a watery realm. Houses collapsed, and people drowned daily. Shops in the city presented a desolate scene. Rice merchants seized the opportunity to manipulate rice prices, selling each斗(dǒu) for more than three dollars. Many middle-class families were forced to eat麦面(mài miàn) wheat noodles once a day. Poor residents could only fill their stomachs with vegetables such as pumpkins and eggplants.

Chongqing: The river water in the city inevitably rises every summer, but it usually recedes quickly with minor damages. However, this year, starting from August 1st, the Yangtze and Jialing Rivers began to rise. On the night of the 5th, they suddenly surged. Residents along the riverbanks were caught unprepared, their houses, food, and utensils all submerged. Some men and women also drowned. A subsequent investigation revealed a total of 500 refugee households, about 3,000 people.

Lu County: After August 3rd, the water levels in the two rivers rose sharply, creating a vast expanse of water as far as the eye could see. Disaster victims received aid from the Red Cross Society, resulting in few deaths. The Red Cross has telegraphed various parties for relief. The telegram roughly stated: "At the confluence of the two rivers in Lu County, the upstream water level rose sharply on the 3rd and 4th. Areas near the city, such as Shuncheng Street and Kaiba Gully, as well as Xiaoshi Xiang on the opposite bank, have become a watery realm. The water rose rapidly, leaving no time for evacuation. Disaster victims are crowding on the city walls, their cries of hunger unbearable to hear. Our society, witnessing this heartbreaking scene, quickly organized a rescue team and set out to provide assistance. Four large river rescue boats and three small river rescue boats are operating day and night, rescuing over a hundred people. Currently, during the summer vacation, all schools are closed. We have contacted schools, using the Lu County Middle School, Lu County Higher Primary School, Lu County Public School, and Lu County Model Primary School as temporary shelters for the disaster victims. We are rushing to make bread and cook thin porridge to distribute to the displaced people. However, the flood disaster is exceptionally severe, unprecedented in recent decades. Even in the areas near the city, there is an urgent need for relief. Moreover, riverside villages such as Yimin, Zhonghou, Chongyi, Fulong, Huiwen, Lire, and Fenghuang Li, where rice paddies have not yet been harvested and soybeans are ripe, have all been submerged. How will the people survive? We earnestly request the allocation of large funds to be distributed to the counties for relief, so that the withered trees can be rejuvenated and the fish in the dried ruts can be revived. This will all be thanks to the benevolence of kind-hearted people."

Neijiang and Fushun: Since the beginning of August, the Tuo River's upstream floodwaters have surged several丈(zhàng), with torrential currents. From Sujiawan, Yinshan Town, Tianxikou, and Lijia Street in Zizhong County, to Jiamu Town, Baima Temple, Shihui Creek, Longmen Town, Niufodu, and Shizi Tan in Neijiang, and to Fushun City, Lijiawan, Huangge Fort, Pipa Chang, Zhaohua Town, Tongtan, and Lianyu Dong, farmland and houses along both banks of the river have been washed away. Only raging waves were visible along the river. The cries for help from men and women clinging to rooftops and tall trees were unbearable to hear. However, due to the massive waves, rescue boats could not get close, so few people were rescued. Property and rice paddies floated away with the current. It is estimated that over ten thousand people drowned, thousands of homes were washed away, property losses amounted to several million, and hundreds of thousands of acres of rice paddies were destroyed, truly an unprecedented disaster.

Hechuan: Since the beginning of August, heavy rain has continued in this county, causing the river water to rise by seven or eight丈(zhàng). The magnitude of the flood is unprecedented in the past ten years. Agricultural products washed away on both banks reached over a hundred里(lǐ). More than a thousand houses were submerged. Farmers helped the old and the young, fleeing to nearby villages and towns. People in the county are working to provide relief. In the urban areas near the river, the people suffered even greater losses. When the water rose, many residents dismantled their houses and moved into the city. About dozens of homes were submerged and washed away because they could not be dismantled in time. Approximately fifty people drowned.

Tongchuan: Since August 2nd, continuous heavy rain has caused the Tong River to rise endlessly. Riverside residents and rice paddies along both banks were submerged, resulting in significant losses. The county's various agencies are organizing a disaster relief association to investigate the affected victims and devise ways to provide assistance.

Jiangjin: On August 4th and 5th, continuous heavy rain caused the river water to surge. Houses along the river were almost completely submerged, leaving ordinary poor people and small merchants with no place to live and no way to survive, crying out to the heavens. The situation was dire. The chamber of commerce has specially set up relief efforts, providing porridge twice a day and appealing to all parties for relief to save the poor people affected by the flood.

Zizhong and Ziyang: Since August 3rd, the Tuo River has risen sharply. Over two hundred里(lǐ)of riverside villages and towns in Zizhong and Ziyang counties have been submerged, turning into a watery realm. Countless fields, houses, crops, livestock, and utensils have been washed away. In particular, ripened grains, whether still flowering or about to flower, have all turned into white husks. Various miscellaneous grains have withered, offering no hope. Tens of thousands of residents have drowned. Although people in both counties are urgently seeking relief, it is like a drop in the bucket, insufficient to address the problem.

Suining: This county is located in the Sichuan Basin, with the Fu River running through it. Every summer and autumn, when the river floods, the banks often suffer, but the floods have not been very severe, and the losses have been minimal. Unexpectedly, at the beginning of August this year, incessant rain caused the Fu River to surge. The water inside the city reached several feet deep. Countless fields and houses along the riverbanks were submerged. In the county seat alone, over a hundred houses were washed away, and over forty people drowned.

The above accounts, though only from over a dozen counties, represent a region throughout Sichuan Province. The number of disaster victims reaches hundreds of thousands, with countless fields and properties lost. After enduring the ravages of war, banditry, and exorbitant taxes, the people of Sichuan are now suffering from a flood disaster, truly an unprecedented catastrophe. (August 17th)

The Breach in the Canal Embankment is Being Repaired 58

Provincial Chairman Ye Chucang Personally Inspects the Disaster in Jiangbei

Construction Department Cables Provinces to Send Personnel to Assist in Rescue Efforts

Zhenjiang Dispatch: The situation of the canal embankment breaches has been investigated from various sources in recent days. Yangzhou and Shaobo have the most breaches, estimated at around fifteen. Fortunately, the Huaipi section near Gaoyou city in the Gao-Bao section is unscathed. The Huailou Bay and Qingshui Tan between Gaoyou and Sishui, known dangerous sections of the canal embankment, miraculously survived this time, which is fortunate. Yesterday, Provincial Chairman Ye Chucang interviewed Director Wu of the Canal Works Department, who had returned to the province from Gaoyou, for details. This morning (31st) at 6:00 AM, he set off with Director Wu of the Relief Committee, Cheng Jingsheng, and others, aboard the Yuanchang Wheel to personally inspect the upstream and downstream areas along the canal, planning to return after reaching Qingjiangpu.

Li Mingyang, Director of the Provincial Security Department, went to Jiangbei on the 28th of this month to inspect and arrived at Qingjiangpu on the 30th. He telegraphed the province yesterday, stating that the water level in the Huaipi section had dropped sharply. He is now rushing back to Gaoyou to find ways to repair the breaches. At the same time, Zhao, the director of the Huaipi section, also telegraphed that Rescue Commissioner Zhang Bin immediately returned to You with personnel, 麻包(mā bāo) burlap sacks, and other materials to repair the breaches. Currently, repairing the canal embankment breaches is of utmost importance. In addition to dispatching personnel to take charge of the rescue efforts and transferring personnel from other locations to assist, the Construction Department also telegraphed the Construction Departments of Shandong, Henan, and Hebei provinces yesterday, requesting the loan of experienced supervisors in damming and embankment work to come to Jiangsu to assist in quickly repairing the breaches.

Regarding the dangerous situation near Shaobo Town in the Jiangdu section, Director Shao telegraphed yesterday that rescue materials had arrived at the site in large quantities and were being rushed to repair the breaches day and night. This morning, the Construction Department sent Chief Engineer Fei Peixiang aboard the Charity Association's small wheel to Shaobo to supervise the construction work at Zhaoguan Dam. Pacification Commissioner Zhang Zhijiang also sent a battalion of soldiers to assist in the rescue efforts. With concentrated effort, significant progress is expected in a short period.

Note: The canal from Huaiyin and Huaian in the south to Jiangdu in the north has an east bank embankment that is higher than the houses, reaching nearly two丈(zhàng). In the event of a major flood, the Yi, Shu, Huai, and Si Rivers pour down directly. To the west are Hongze, Baoying, Gaoyou, and Shaobo Lakes, about a hundred里(lǐ) wide and four hundred里(lǐ) long. The turbulent waves冲击(chōng jī) pound, connecting the rivers and lakes. All rely on a single east embankment for protection. This time, with fifteen breaches between Gao and Shao, lake water poured out like a rapid waterfall. The rooftops and treetops were mostly submerged, and the devastation can be imagined. Moreover, the area is all plains, with no high ground. There is nowhere to escape when the flood comes. All counties, including Gaoxing, Jiangbao, Taidong, Yanfu, etc., each spanning hundreds of里(lǐ) in all directions, are now suffering this calamity. The loss of life and property is incalculable. This map is drawn to illustrate the situation.

Repair Work Near Wanshou Palace Has Been Completed

Various Agencies Are Busy Assessing the Disaster and Providing Relief

Yangzhou Dispatch: The disaster situation of the dike breaches in Shaobo and Gaoyou has been detailed in previous reports. It is now known that the water in Shaobo has gradually receded. As of the 30th, it had dropped eight尺(chǐ) compared to its deepest level. The breach is now being repaired by Shao Fuchen, the director of the Jiangdu section, who arrived on the 29th aboard the Xinbaoyuan Wheel, loaded with 江柴(jiāng chái) Jiang-made materials. One breach near Wanshou Palace has been completed today (30th), and the second is being repaired, which is expected to be completed tonight. The news of fundraising and disaster assessment from various parties is excerpted below: (1) The Jiangsu Charity Association has sent Relief Director Yuan Xiaogu and Executive Committee Member Cao Songqiao to investigate the disaster situation in six counties, including Yangzhou. Upon arriving in the town and learning of the Shaogao dike breaches, they hired six small wheels and ten sailing boats and arrived at the Green Willow Hotel in Yangzhou on the 29th. They met with Yang Shengwu, a standing committee member of the Jiangdu Emergency Relief Association, and decided to set up a temporary office in Yangzhou to establish shelters and send all boats and wheels to distribute relief and rescue lives in the Gao-Shao-Xinghua area. (2) The Zhenjiang Navigation Association telegraphed the Emergency Relief Association here, saying that all dispatched wheels and tugboats have not returned to the town, making it difficult to continue. Please ask the Emergency Relief Group to find a way to release several wheels urgently to load and transport the Charity Association's food for relief. (3) The Shanghai Yangzhou Native Place Association sent 2,000 yuan to Ruan Mubai's contribution to the disaster relief fund on the 30th, for the use of the Emergency Relief Association. (4) The Ningbo Native Place Association in Yangzhou held an emergency meeting, recommending Wang Jingao and Feng Buqing to go to the disaster area for investigation. (5) Emergency Relief Association Chairman Wang Jingtang went to Gaoyou on the 29th for disaster relief and returned to Yangzhou late at night, bringing back more than a thousand refugees. Disaster Victims in Shaobo Carrying Baskets Begging for Food

Detailed Record of the Dike Collapse at the North Gate of Gaoyou 60

Most of the Houses Were Washed Away

Over Ten Thousand People Died Tragically

Water Inside the City is Eight尺(chǐ) Deep

Refugees Crowding at the South Gate

Gaoyou Dispatch: As of noon on the 25th, the water level in the canal of this county had dropped to one丈(zhàng) nine尺(chǐ). Initially, it was believed that there would be no further danger, so the authorities had stopped the work in an intangible way. Unexpectedly, at 7:00 PM that afternoon, a northeast wind suddenly rose, and the canal dike became slightly strained, but no one defended it. Around midnight, the wind suddenly turned northwest, followed by torrential rain, and huge waves directly衝刷(chōng shuā) pounded the dike. It was extremely dangerous. At this time, a jailbreak occurred in the county prison, with seventeen criminals escaping. The police team fired shots to pursue and capture them, while simultaneously closing the four city gates. Twelve people were captured, and five escaped. Because it was late at night, the residents inside the city heard gunshots and suspected that bandits had entered the city, causing great panic. Unexpectedly, at that time, the water suddenly overflowed at three locations: Miaoxiangkou, Yumatou, and Tonghu Bridge at the North Gate. Nearby residents sounded the alarm, but the North Gate was tightly closed due to the jailbreak, and the alarm could not enter the city. It was not until 1:30 AM on the 26th that the city gate was opened, and the alarm was able to enter the city. However, all shops and households suspected that bandits were using a trick, so they did not dare to open their doors. Therefore, although the alarm sounded everywhere, except for County Magistrate Wang and a few laborers on the canal embankment, no one from the shops, employees, and residents held high pole lanterns to defend the dike. The situation became helpless without lights for taking soil and rescue work. At Miaoxiangkou, Yumatou, and Tonghu Bridge, the new and old子埝(zǐ niàn) dams, which were three to four尺(chǐ) high, collapsed, each about ten餘丈(yú zhàng) in length. The water flowed directly east (Picture of dike breach at Lotus Pond, Gaoyou) like a dam was opened. Residents outside the city supported the old and carried the young, crying and weeping, and entered the city to take refuge. A small number of residents, unwilling to abandon their homes, built water pavilions and climbed up to avoid the water. After the refugees entered the city, they closed the North Gate. Unexpectedly, in less than two hours, the houses in Miaoxiangkou, Kongxin Street, and Tonghu Bridge at the North Gate were completely washed away by the water, as they were the first to bear the brunt. At this time, there was great chaos at Beishikou. All shops were looted by the poor people. The merchants in the city learned the news and immediately arrested more than ten people and sent them to the county for punishment. The market order was restored. By 7:00 AM, the North Gate area and East Street were also eight尺(chǐ) deep in water. At one time, nine out of ten houses outside the city were submerged and collapsed. Many residents drowned. Suddenly, floating corpses filled the water, flowing directly eastward, with the most miserable conditions. Many residents, seeing the rapid water, wanted to enter the city urgently but were unable to do so, so they went to Chengtian Temple Qianfo Building for refuge. However, more and more people came here to take refuge, and the pressure was too great. Qianfo Building collapsed as a result. It is said that more than a thousand people were crushed to death, which is truly tragic. At 9:00 AM, the Shuiguan at the North Gate also leaked, causing more and more panic among the people. Residents in the city also built water pavilions. By 11:00 AM, because the rescue work was ineffective, the streets in the city gradually had water. At this time, ordinary residents rushed to buy dry food and went to the city walls or water pavilions to avoid the water. At that time, the food shops were sold out. Around 1:00 AM on the 27th, because the northwest wind was very strong, Liangshiwu at the south of city twenty-five里(lǐ) and Xiaolubao in Yangzhou Prefecture suddenly collapsed, each about twenty or thirty丈(zhàng). The water level of the canal decreased significantly. The existing water level is about one丈(zhàng) six尺(chǐ). However, because the Shuiguan at the North Gate was never blocked, the deepest part of the city had reached eight尺(chǐ), and the shallowest part was about one尺(chǐ). Therefore, the residents in the city have been escaping to the South Gate, half of them hiring boats to live on the water, and the other half camping on the canal dike. It was a scene of crying, which was unbearable to hear. County Magistrate Wang believes that the water in the city is very high and will continue to rise, and he sent all the prisoners, more than two hundred, to Yangzhou by boat this afternoon (27th) to be temporarily placed in the county prison. Currently, Gaoyou City has limited food, and the people are about to starve. Moreover, the downstream water is also逼(bī) pressing the city, which is very dangerous. If the relief associations do not quickly send rescue boats to Gaoyou for relief, all the people in the city may perish together. Gaoyou City has suffered this disaster, which is unprecedented. (August 27th)

Another report: Wang Long, the magistrate of Gaoyou County, has escorted all the prisoners to Yangzhou for detention. It is said that they have been transferred to Zhenjiang.

Overview of Flood Disaster in Various Counties of Hubei (Continued) 61

Guangji: Due to the flooding of the Yangtze River in the county, the eighteen surrounding areas outside the Luocheng Dike, including Liu, Guo, Jia, Dai, Du, Zhou, Daoyang, Xifan, and Lujiao, were all flooded. By August 1st, the Luocheng Dike was breached, and the forty-eight surrounding areas inside the dike were also breached. As a result, villages such as Tongsi, Dongsan, Zhongsan, and Xisi were turned into a watery realm, with depths of over one丈(zhàng) in some places and several尺(chǐ) in others. People's houses were all in the water, and the suffering was truly difficult to count. (Relief measures) Temporarily allocated 276石(dàn) of relief rice and telegraphed the Emergency Relief Association to find ways to provide relief.

Huangmei: Before the Liu Zuokou section of the river embankment in the county was breached, incessant rain had lasted for months. All the dams were submerged by accumulated water. Disaster victims in various districts requested permits to leave the area, and their situation was extremely tragic. When the Qilu and Jingjiang Dikes in Susong were breached, Liu Zuokou was also breached. The Yangtze River flood poured into the county from this breach. The people in various民埦(mín wǎn) villages in the county, such as Wangjia Daxu and Panxingxu, and all forty-eight圩(wéi) weirs in the county, were successively breached without exception. The county seat area was also flooded. In total, more than two-thirds of the county became a watery realm, with over 200,000 disaster victims. (Relief measures) Temporarily allocated 200石(dàn) of relief rice and telegraphed the Emergency Relief Association to find ways to provide relief.

Yangxin: The county is located on the Yangtze River and has no堤防(dī fáng) embankments. Since spring, the water level has risen sharply. The northeast and central districts have turned into a watery realm. In addition, mountain torrents erupted, and continuous rain fell. In late July, more than 200 people died from the heat, the scorching sun, and starvation. No less than 50 people died from being crushed by collapsing houses. Those who escaped to high ground were harassed by Red bandits. Currently, tens of thousands of disaster victims gather outside the county government every day, wailing and appealing for relief. (Relief measures) Temporarily allocated 200石(dàn) of relief rice and telegraphed the Emergency Relief Association to find ways to provide relief.

Shishou: The county is divided into five districts. The northeast districts are entirely within the 赤化(chì huà) communized zone and have not been planted. The Gu, Xing, Yong, Gong, He, Xing, Yi Dikes and Zhang, Hui, Quan, Nan and Liu He were breached. In the central, southwest and south districts, only high-lying cities and a small number of houses can still be seen. The farmland has all turned into a watery realm. In total, it is estimated that 60 to 70 percent of the county has been affected by the disaster. (Relief measures) Temporarily allocated 600石(dàn) of relief rice and telegraphed the Emergency Relief Association to find ways to provide relief.

Tianmen: The county was originally divided into five districts. Except for the northern district, which is located in a mountainous area and was spared from the flood, the eastern, western, southern, and central districts were affected by the breaches in the Yangjia Yue and Deng Liwan on the Bianxiang River; the breaches in the Tanjia Yuan and Baihu Yuan on the Niu蹄(tí) hoof branch river; and the breaches in the Sigang under Qianjiang on the county river. As a result, places such as Yu Fan, Heishi, Xia Zhou, Henghe, and Linggou, as well as the county's 72 垸(yuàn) surrounding embankments and the Tanjia Yuan and Baihu Yuan in the second district, have all turned into a watery realm. There is almost no way to travel in the eastern, western, and southern villages. Houses collapsed, and people and livestock drowned. The areas outside the disaster zone were also flooded by accumulated water. In total, it is estimated that 80 percent of the county has been affected by the flood, with over 600,000 people affected. (Relief measures) Temporarily allocated 200石(dàn) of relief rice and telegraphed the Emergency Relief Association to find ways to provide relief.

Jiangling: Since the beginning of summer, the county has experienced continuous rain and high底水(dǐ shuǐ) base water levels. Later, there were more than ten days of heavy rain, with the water level in the plains reaching several尺(chǐ). In addition, the Yangtze River and inland lakes rose at the same time, and areas such as Cenhekou turned into a watery realm. In addition to being affected by breaches in Qianjiang, Tianjing 剅(dōu), etc., the county suffered both internal and external damage. There is no hope for the autumn harvest. The flood in Longwan was the worst, followed by Bushe and Hao Hu. In total, it is estimated that two-thirds of the county has been affected by the disaster. (Relief measures) Temporarily allocated 200石(dàn) of relief rice and telegraphed the Emergency Relief Association to find ways to provide relief.

Xin Chun: First and subsequently, the Yongbao and Yonggu dikes breached. Total of 52 breaches including Maoshan Dike, Dingfeng Dike, and Lijia Zhou, the Chidong Lake Guanshan enclosure with an area of about 80余里(yú lǐ). The autumn rice harvest was suddenly submerged. The harvest was failed. Houses and buildings were almost completely collapsed. Many people and animals were drowned because they were unable to escape. Thousands of households are awaiting food. (Relief measures) Telegraphed the Emergency Relief Association and requested relief.

Echeng: Over 60 breaches of the dike in Erfangwan. The farmland in the Dayang and Yezhou areas that was flooded reached over 100,000畝(mǔ). Thousands of houses collapsed. The Piplake Dike burst, and it is estimated that 3,000畝(mǔ) of rice seedlings and cotton were submerged, and over 200 houses were washed away. The Chenhu Dike, Tangbiaoshu Dike, and Shajiahu Dike also breached successively. People were displaced and in great distress. (Relief measures) Telegraphed the Emergency Relief Association and requested relief.

Min Ribao Assault Case 62

Various Circles Scheduled an Emergency Meeting

Fuzhou Dispatch: After various circles decided to refuse to read Japanese people in Fujian's news, at 5:00 PM on August 24, the Union of Maritime Workers sent instructor Pan Hongwen and staff member Wu Zantong to the Min Ribao newspaper office to persuade the printing workers to stop working because they received a notice from the Anti-Japanese Association. Unexpectedly, the newspaper office was heavily guarded by the Japanese. Hearing that members of the Union of Maritime Workers were visiting, a Taiwanese staff member disguised himself as a Chinese person to greet them. Pan Hongwen instructed Wu Zantong to wait in front of the door while he went inside to negotiate. The Taiwanese asked about their intentions and, upon learning that they were urging a strike, instigated the staff members to surround and violently beat him. Seeing that the situation was not good in front of the door, Wu Zantong hurried in to dissuade them. Pan was able to escape in the meantime. Seeing that Pan had left, the staff members imprisoned Wu. As of 12:00 AM on August 25, members of the Union of Maritime Workers, together with the chief of the 5th district and the police, searched the vicinity of the Min Ribao newspaper office but could not find any trace of him. Therefore, his life or death is unknown. After Pan escaped, he fainted on the ground after taking a few steps because of his serious injuries. Residents carried him to the 5th district, where Chief Shao Zhicheng briefly questioned him and then sent the police to escort him to the Union of Maritime Workers. The union hired Western-trained doctor Liao Pinfang to treat him. It was found that his lungs and intestines were seriously injured, his fever was high, and he was unconscious. He was given an injection to calm his nerves and relieve the pain. At that time, members of the Union of Maritime Workers rushed to visit him upon hearing the news. Seeing the situation, they were extremely angry and wanted to go to the Min Ribao newspaper office for serious negotiations. The staff of the union and the chief of the 5th district persuaded them to stop. On the morning of the 25th, Pan Hongwen's injuries worsened, he vomited blood, his voice was hoarse, and he vomited soon after drinking. Then, the Union of Maritime Workers carried him back to his home in Linghou. However, members of the Union of Maritime Workers were determined to deal severely with the Min Ribao newspaper office because one person was missing and the other was dying. They gathered in the union to plan the method, and the atmosphere was extremely tense. After receiving the report, the Anti-Japanese Association also believed that the matter was serious and decided to hold an emergency meeting at 2:00 PM on the 25th to discuss everything. Local newspapers have published huge headlines about this matter, and society is paying close attention. The attitude of the Min Ribao newspaper office is still calm, or it has something to rely on. (August 25th)

Inauguration of the Fourth Zhejiang Provincial Congress 63

A preparatory meeting was held after the opening ceremony yesterday.

Hangzhou Dispatch: The Fourth Zhejiang Provincial Congress was inaugurated at 9 a.m. on August 31st. The Central Government sent Zhang Daofan to attend and provide guidance. Guests attending the ceremony included Zhang Nanxian, Fang Ce, Zhang Naiyan, Zheng Tian, Xu Baoju, and others, totaling over 200 people. Executive and Supervisory Committee members attending included Xu Shaodi, Ye Suzhong, Chen Xihao, and others, along with 155 delegates such as Wu Wangji. Xu Shaodi presided over the meeting and delivered the opening address after the ceremony. He first emphasized the importance of the current congress and expressed his hopes, followed by these points: (1) All comrades should seek knowledge at any time and place to increase revolutionary strength; (2) Each comrade should lead the people by setting an example everywhere. Zhang Daofan then delivered an instructional speech on behalf of the Central Government: (1) He hoped that Zhejiang comrades would unite and continue their revolutionary efforts under a shared belief; (2) The Central Government sincerely hoped that Zhejiang comrades would consider matters from a long-term and broader perspective, and not create party disputes due to personal or minority self-interest or emotional impulses; (3) Electing the fourth session of the Provincial Executive and Supervisory Committee members is also one of the important events of this congress, and he hoped that everyone would elect loyal comrades to take on the heavy responsibility of party affairs. Finally, Provincial Governor Zhang Nanxian and Committee member Fang Ce delivered speeches. The preparatory meeting was held at 2 p.m. to elect the presidium chairman of the congress and members of various committees. The election results for the presidium chairman were Wu Wangji, Gu Youmin, and Yu Lie, who were elected.

Local Dispatches

Baoshan 64

The Baoshan seawall is in a very dangerous state. This year, floods have occurred almost all over the country. The Baoshan seawall also collapsed in several places during the hurricane and heavy rain on August 26. Fortunately, the northeast wind turned northwest that evening, preventing a disaster. However, it was still a close call. If the wind had not changed direction, the collapse of the seawall would have turned Baoshan, not to mention Shanghai, Jiading, Taicang, Qingpu, and Kunshan counties, into a swamp, and all would have become fish in a pond. The immediate danger has passed, but who knows if future storms will not be more severe than today's? It is up to the authorities and local people to manage the aftermath well.

Suzhou 65

Bandit traces discovered in Dongting East Mountain. Chief Shen of the Water Police Third District reported that bandit traces were discovered in Dongting East Mountain on the morning of the 31st. After receiving the report, Chief Shen immediately dispatched the Zhizhong motorboat, towing four patrol boats, to handle the matter in the afternoon.

Building dikes and repairing city walls. The Wuxian Agricultural and Commercial Associations believe that Wuxian County is located in a water village and that there are no dikes in the villages. Once there is continuous rain, the low-lying fields are extremely dangerous. Therefore, they have specially petitioned the county government to forward the request to the Construction Department to suspend construction for one year and use all construction funds for building dikes. Yesterday, Bureau Chief Qian of the Construction Bureau sent a letter to local gentry Zhang Zhongren, asking for his advocacy on this matter. Repairing the city walls is also an urgent matter, and he also asked for advocacy to gain the sympathy of local people.

Fengxian 66

The county government reports on the wind disaster situation. County Magistrate Shen Qingchen, currently addressing the losses from the wind disaster, reported to the provincial authorities yesterday requesting an inspection. He stated that starting from the 26th of this month, the county suddenly experienced strong winds and heavy rain, which lasted for two days and nights before subsiding. It was found that the cotton was in the boll-forming stage, and after this blow, it was almost entirely scattered. Most of the rice was still flowering, and after this disaster, it would be showy but not fruitful. The prospects for the autumn harvest are hopeless. Furthermore, countless houses and sheds in the villages have collapsed. Along the seawall, the tide rose sharply, and huge waves crashed against it. Not only were the floodgates submerged, but also many of the newly reclaimed sandy beaches were flooded. Thinking of the people's livelihood, he felt deeply chilled. In addition to consulting with the district chiefs to properly devise remedial measures, he reported the situation and requested relief.

Songjiang 67

筹设水灾筹振会议

筹设水灾筹振会议。 The various circles of the county are deeply sympathetic, and the county government convened a meeting today (31st) to prepare for a flood relief meeting. The leaders of the various agencies and bureau chiefs attended, with County Magistrate Shen presiding, reporting on the process of convening the meeting. It was decided to appoint the county magistrate as the chairman of the committee, and the education bureau, the county chamber of commerce, the pacification headquarters, the county party headquarters, the Songjin Daily, and other seven agencies as standing committee members, and the district chiefs as ex officio members. In the future, the methods of fundraising will be determined separately by all sectors of society, such as the business community raising funds through the Chamber of Commerce, and local gentry and wealthy people raising funds through the district chiefs. The amount of relief funds raised will be reported immediately, and the office will be located in the county government. Currently, the business community is very enthusiastic about the relief funds.

Wuxi 68

The relief association was established yesterday. The county party headquarters and the county chamber of commerce, considering that the flood in Jiangbei had caused widespread suffering, urgently needed relief, and convened people from all walks of life at the county chamber of commerce at 3 p.m. yesterday (31st) for an emergency meeting to discuss relief measures. Chairman Qian Sunqing first reported on the situation, and then the discussion began: 1. It was decided to name the organization the Wuxi County Relief Association, which was established immediately; 2. The cadre council was organized by the party headquarters, the county government, the county chamber of commerce, and other 13 agencies and groups; 3. Tang Weizhi and Hua Yishan were publicly elected as chairman and vice chairman.

A red pill dealer threw himself into the river after being swindled. Li Sifa from Qingshiqiao, outside the North Gate, purchased 3,000 red pills from Ji Ju at Dahechi Yantou on the 29th to resell to customers. However, after unpacking and inspecting them, they were not genuine. Li immediately held a knife and asked Ji to exchange them, but Ji refused. Initially, they argued verbally, then they fought. Finally, Li was wrestled by Ji and thrown into the nearby Yantoutou Creek, where he drowned himself. Li died on the spot. Seeing that he had caused a disaster, Ji fled immediately. Later, people fished Li out and rescued him using artificial respiration, but his breath was barely sustained and negotiations are still underway.

Raising funds for emergency relief for the Jiangbei flood. The Jiangbei flood is extremely severe. After receiving an urgent telegram from the provincial government, the Wuxi county government consulted with the chamber of commerce and invited the New Zhen, Fei Peng, New Yufu, and New Qingrui and other four steamers, as well as eight civilian boats, and dispatched police squad leader Li Shanga on the 29th to escort them to Zhenjiang to await dispatch to the disaster area. That evening, the provincial government continued to send committee members to Wuxi, saying that the disaster area was vast and there were many victims, and that the steamers already requisitioned were difficult to use and that another 20 steamers and tugboats needed to be hired and limited to Zhenjiang. County Magistrate Chen has tasked committees to search everywhere. Yesterday afternoon, two steamers, four large motorboats, and more than ten civilian boats were rented and sent to Zhenjiang first.

The court thoroughly investigates the case of a rebellious son killing his father. In Zhengjia Lane, Wan'an City, the sixteenth district of the county, there was a case of a rebellious son, Zheng Chunquan, killing his father, Zheng Genda. The chief prosecutor of the county court, Zhou Erkai, dispatched police chief Li Renzhen to the countryside to investigate secretly after receiving a report. After learning the facts, he summoned the rebellious son Chunquan and his mother Zhang to the town office that night to inquire about the truth. Chunquan firmly refused to admit it. Zhang, deeply protecting her son, claimed that she had broken Genda's head with a smoking pipe due to a minor argument, and firmly refused to confess to Chunquan's actions. Therefore, police chief Li escorted the rebellious son Chunquan and Zhang to the city together. Chief Prosecutor Zhou opened a court to investigate and went to the countryside yesterday to open the coffin for an autopsy, to be handled according to the law.

Silk public bonds issued today. The Wuxi silk mill trade association convened a temporary members' meeting the day before yesterday (29th) to discuss how to receive the public bonds. Representatives from more than 30 silk mills attended. Chairman Qian Fenghao first reported that the four million yuan in bonds for silk industry public bonds for Jiangsu and Zhejiang had been issued by the Ministry of Finance and Industry and handed over to the Silk Industry Public Bond Fund Management Committee for collection. Except for Longchang Silk Mill outside Dongmen, Xishan Silk Mill in Miaogang, and Youcheng Silk Mill under Wu Qiao, which had ceased operations before the silk industry public bonds were initiated, and therefore had no right to receive the public bonds, the remaining mills could fill in the amount according to the roster and the association would issue a certificate, which would be stamped by the person and then taken to the Shanghai Jiangsu and Zhejiang Silk Industry Public Bond Fund Management Committee to verify the certificate and check that the seals matched. After filling out a written guarantee, they could receive the ticket amount at the Trust Department of the National Goods Bank at No. 3 Hankou Road, Shanghai, from 9 a.m. to 12 p.m. and 2 p.m. to 5 p.m. starting on August 31st. After the report, the representatives carefully discussed and decided that each factory would automatically obtain the certificate from the association in the near future and then go to Shanghai to receive the public bonds. After the meeting, one thief was captured in a robbery. Xu Renquan, a villager from Laoxu Lane, south of Furong Mountain (Tianshi City) in the sixth district, was a farmer with a modest family fortune. At 12 o'clock the night before, more than a dozen thieves suddenly came, each holding a weapon, and broke open the gate with huge stones and rushed in. Renquan's younger brother, A Mei, immediately climbed onto the roof, jumped into the neighbor's house, and sounded the gong to gather the crowd. The thieves heard the sound of the gong and knew that the villagers were prepared, so they scrambled in the mulberry field. After hearing the alarm, the villagers bravely captured a thief on the spot, wielding farm implements. He was sent to the Eleventh Branch of the Public Security Bureau under its jurisdiction. After a strict interrogation by Branch Chief Li, the thief confessed his name as Mao Er, from Chang'an Bridge, and admitted to the robbery of the Xu family. Li verified the confession and submitted a document to the headquarters yesterday for investigation.

Changzhou 69

A renowned bandit who surrendered still engages in illegal activities. Shang Changsheng, a renowned bandit from Caojiaba, Laogu Bridge, in the northern countryside of Wu County, had previously asked someone to submit a surrender request to the county government. County Magistrate Zhang, considering that the bandit had illegal activities, secretly ordered the detective team leader Ni Gusheng to go and arrest him. Team Leader Ni immediately went with Captain Peng of the First Squadron and First Team of the police. When they arrived at Shang Changsheng's house, bandits Xiao Changzhou (Shi Quansheng), Yichitou (Shun Da), Zhang Hongsheng, and others suddenly rushed out and opened fire to resist arrest. The police team chased after them and returned fire. However, they were hindered by the fields and trenches in the countryside, and the bandits took advantage of the cover to escape by swimming in the river. They failed to capture them. When they returned to investigate, Shang Changsheng had also disappeared. Team Leader Ni reported the situation to the county government for approval on the 30th.

Zhenjiang 70

The relief committee mortgaged construction public bonds. The Jiangsu Provincial Relief Committee held a relief meeting in the office of the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs at 2 p.m. yesterday. Those present included Wang Yiting, Cheng Jingsheng, He Yushu, Lu Xiaobo, Ye Chucang, Hu Puan, and Xu Baoying. The discussion items included a resolution to request Wang Yiting to take 1 million construction public bonds to Shanghai to mortgage for relief funds, with a minimum amount of 200,000 yuan. As the amount of relief funds for each county had not yet been determined, they could not be distributed immediately. After the meeting, Wang Yiting took the 5:49 special express train to Shanghai to discuss everything.

The Jiangsu Construction Department will divide construction zones. The Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department, in order to promote the balanced development of construction projects in various counties, intends to divide construction zones and convene construction supervisors from various counties for a meeting in the province. It is rumored that it was decided to divide Wuxi, Wu County, and other seven counties into one zone, with a trial run planned for next month. However, it is rumored that local people in various counties believe that the funding varies in each region, and the needs of the projects also vary from place to place. In the future, the zoning of construction will create a situation in which resources are diverted from one place to another in terms of funding, and in terms of projects, there will be concerns about ineffectiveness. The so-called balanced development will be nothing but empty words. Moreover, at a time of widespread floods in the province, after the establishment of this type of construction zone, if the existing construction bureaus are all abolished, the talents in the zone organs may not be as familiar with the local situation as the personnel in the original construction bureaus. The repairs of river works and embankment projects will inevitably result in losses in both economy and time due to the unfamiliarity with the situation. Therefore, the public opinion of local people in various counties in recent days often calls for opposition.

Kunshan 71

Gamblers resisted arrest and beat the police. In Yingfengqiao and other villages in the seventh district of the county, gambling is prevalent. Teahouses are lined up, and scoundrels gather to lure honest people into gambling. The local area suffers greatly. On the 28th of this month, the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau dispatched police to arrest them. However, the general gamblers disregarded the police and rose up to resist arrest. Seeing the situation was unfavorable, the police tried to escape, but the illegal gamblers dared to hold farm implements and block them and beat them severely. Three policemen were seriously injured. Now, Branch Chief Jiang Zhaokun is ordering the village chiefs and heads to hand over all the perpetrators and send them to the county for investigation.

Jiangyin 72

The tragic situation after the dike collapse in the Third District. The Third District borders the Yangtze River. Last month, continuous rain and rising tides made the rice and cotton in the fields almost hopeless. Since the sudden arrival of the hurricane on the 25th, the tide has risen sharply by several feet, and the dikes of each enclosed land have been precarious. As night fell, the wind intensified, and the dikes along the river collapsed one after another. The tide rushed into the enclosed land through the breaches, with surging waves. The water depth in each enclosed land was five or six feet. Many victims climbed trees or rooftops, wailing for help. The situation was unbearable. The most severely affected areas were Zhicheng, Chongsan, Dongya, and Jiahe and other villages, a vast expanse of water. Among the deaths were Chen Jinshen's eighty-year-old mother, who was crushed to death by a house, Tao Gengchu's wife and two sons and two daughters, and a seventeen-year-old girl surnamed Shen, who were all drowned. In total, over 20,000 mu of farmland were affected, and 3,000 to 4,000 people were affected. There was widespread mourning, and people were crying out for food. Xu Kuiqing, the head of the Third District, urgently reported to County Magistrate Peng and telegraphed the flood relief organization for emergency relief to save the people.

Nantong 73

Relief for flood victims in Jiangbei along the canal. The floods in Gaoyou, Xinghua, and Dongtai counties in Jiangbei are extremely severe. The provincial government has set up a Jiangbei flood victim shelter in Nantong and appointed Xu Zhao to come to Nantong to consult with the county government and the chamber of commerce. On the 30th, they first chartered 60 civilian boats to sail to the disaster area to rescue the victims to Nantong. All inland river boats were transferred to Xingdong to rescue the refugees from danger. The Chamber of Commerce held an emergency meeting to do its best to provide relief to the Jiangbei floods, and first raised 30,000 yuan in relief funds. Yuan Lengyu telegraphed the Chamber of Commerce from Dongtai on the 30th, saying that Xinghua flood victims have been sent to Nantong for shelter by boat. About 2,000 refugees have arrived in the first batch. The Nantong County Chamber of Commerce has set up an office for sheltering flood victims, and empty houses and temples in the city and suburbs are all used as shelters.

Nantong, Haimen, and Qidong textile factories will merge. The textile factories in Nantong, Haimen, and Qidong counties will merge. Starting from September 1st, each factory will jointly handle the sale of cotton and yarn. In the future, profits and losses will be shared, and the economy will be jointly maintained. Public security funding does not need to be reviewed by the party headquarters. The county government reported to the public security bureau whether the revenue and expenditure of the public security branches should be sent to the party headquarters for review. On the 30th, the provincial government issued an order stating that the general chapter of the party does not give the district supervisory committee the power to review the expenses of administrative organs at the same level. The provincial and county supervisory committees only have the power to audit the policy directions and achievements of the government at the same level to see if they are based on the party's program and policies. The state council has the competent authorities for financial review.

Cargo ship encounters danger, multiple deaths by drowning. Yesterday, neighboring boats salvaged the bodies of a mother and daughter, which were handled by the local Water Conservancy Bureau and the Township Office. There are still three male bodies that have not been salvaged.

The disaster situation of rice and cotton in the southeastern villages. The wind and rain caused the most damage to Zixia, Datong, and Heshangsanbang in the southern villages. A total of five or six thousand mu of ripe rice paddies were submerged. Secondly, the cotton fields in the sandy land of Nanyang, Xiaosibu, Jingjiangdian, and other places in the eastern villages collapsed and were submerged for over 20,000 mu. The total income of the county was reduced by a considerable amount.

Business tax revenue is insufficient. Since the business tax in Wan Province began to be prepared in February and levied in June, the revenue has been unusually low. According to the recent statistics from the Department of Finance, as of the 22nd of this month, a total of 32,600 yuan has been collected in the 28 districts of the province, including more than 8,200 yuan in June, more than 16,440 yuan in July, and more than 7,000 yuan in August. The expenses of the bureaus in each district totaled more than 40,000 yuan.

Education News

Highlights

Fifth Anniversary of the National Language Education Promotion Association 77

Nanjing, 31st: The National Mandarin Education Promotion Association held its fifth anniversary conference on the morning of the 1st. Wu Zhihui and other celebrities were invited to give speeches, and a summer phonetic symbol training class and a certificate-giving ceremony for the phonetic symbol training institute were held.

Summary of Correspondence Training Measures for Teachers in Various Counties of Jiangsu 78

The situation of teacher training in various counties of Jiangsu has been reported in previous newspapers. Here is a summary of the department's correspondence training measures: (1) The curriculum is divided into basic education subjects (including six types such as Introduction to Education and Rural Education), education administration subjects (including four types such as Education Administration and Children's Life Guidance), education method subjects (including four types of modern education methods, including elementary school curriculum objectives, homework, and implementation methods, a total of eight types, as well as complex education methods and social education implementation methods), education practice, and discussion of practical problems in elementary school education. If students have unclear basic knowledge of Mandarin, arithmetic, common sense, party principles, etc., they can raise questions at any time and the department will provide practical answers. (2) The meaning of the meaning is that experts in education are hired to edit, and the materials are appropriate, concise, and free of useless, obsolete, and empty materials. (3) The guidance adopts the spirit of the Dalton system and is based on the principle of combining learning and teaching. It divides subjects, stipulates homework guidance and research problems, and uses methods such as questions and answers, tests, investigations, experiments, visits, discussions, and practical exercises to conduct practical research. In addition to the local education bureau coordinating supervision, traveling instructors are hired to travel around to guide in person. (4) The assessment is divided into three types: usual homework, periodic assessment, and graduation examination. (5) The deadline for the training period is limited to one year. (6) Treatment: The original education position (elementary school teacher) is still held concurrently during the training period. Those who pass the training period examination are given priority to be assigned to schools by the original county education bureau. (7) Rewards: Those with excellent results will be given bonuses or prizes and introduced to work in appropriate schools if requested. Those who graduate and pass the examination will be given a graduation certificate. (8) Tuition: Each person is charged 12 yuan for training fees and lecture notes. The fees paid are either subsidized in part or in full by the education bureau, or provided by the students themselves, as determined by the education bureau of each county. However, all fees must be paid in full when the education bureau sends the registration and cannot be refunded midway. The deadline for enrollment for students from provinces and counties other than Jiangsu is extended to the end of September.

The Future of Yangzhou Middle School Students 79

Since its establishment four years ago, the Jiangsu Provincial Yangzhou Middle School has achieved remarkable results through the efforts of Principal Zhou Houku and all the staff and teachers, and has gained a prominent reputation in the domestic secondary education community. The school's moral education and teaching emphasize rigor and practicality, and there are many kinds of extracurricular activities for students, which are guided by full-time teachers in groups, with the aim of striving for social service and promoting the national spirit. In the past, when the school participated in various provincial competitions and exhibitions, the results were among the best. Recently, such as the Boy Scouts sports, have won the championship honor. The head of the Education Department and secretary inspected the school's various moral education facilities and gave many awards. Graduates of the school in the past have generally been able to pass the entrance examinations of famous universities in the country and participate in various examinations. Those who serve in the local elementary education community in the normal department are able to take responsibility and work hard, and are valued by all parties. There are no unemployed graduates. Recently, more than 80 graduates of the general department in this year's summer vacation have been admitted to the Central Jiaotong, Tsinghua, Zhejiang, Wuhan, Jinan, Jinling Universities, and Qinghan Education Fund Measurement and Verification Personnel Aviation School, Central Political School and other places. More than 70 graduates of this year's normal department have also been hired by all parties, especially those serving in elementary schools in the capital and provincial capitals. It is also heard that the school has added a civil engineering department this year, and Principal Zhou has also made considerable arrangements with provincial and county construction agencies for the future of its students. The school currently has 26 classes of high school, junior high school, and rural normal students, with 1,200 students, and nearly 2,000 students including the Experimental Elementary School and the Jingshi Experimental Elementary School. All the school's facilities strive to be down-to-earth, research and progress, and do not advocate novelty to gain a false reputation, so it can achieve unique results.

Opening News of Suzhou Soochow One Middle School 80
