Survey and Repair of the Songkou Seawall 165

Requires 150,000 Yuan

After the seawall in the Wusongkou Baoshan area was damaged by the tide on the night of August 25, although emergency repairs were made, the danger is still very worrying. Yesterday, Zhao Enju, the magistrate of Baoshan County, convened a special meeting of various agencies to discuss the issue. It was proposed to request the provincial government to allocate a huge sum of money for the Seawall Engineering Office to repair it seriously in order to strengthen the seawall and avoid disasters. It was resolved that the local agencies would send telegrams to the provincial government, requesting the immediate allocation of 150,000 yuan for emergency repairs and the formulation of a thorough repair plan. At the same time, Gu Zhenyi, Ji Zhonghe, and Pu Weirun were elected to go to the province to petition, and a seawall protection committee was organized. Then at 2 p.m. yesterday, Magistrate Zhao, together with Xue Zhaoshu, director of the Seawall Engineering Office, and Tan Juenong, director of the Construction Bureau, and Wang Qingtao, the head of the First District, went to the seawall to conduct an on-site inspection. The Wusong Fortress's various forts are built along the seawall, so this time they were also damaged a lot. In addition to reporting to the Ministry of Military Affairs to send personnel to inspect, Commander Deng also sent letters to the Seawall Engineering Office and the Shanghai Public Works Bureau yesterday, requesting joint emergency repairs, and sent his adjutant Li Tang to make contact in person. The northern and southern forts of the fortress are within the scope of the municipal government, while the Shizilin Fort is under the jurisdiction of Baoshan County. The length of the damaged sections along the seawall and the dangerous situation of the existing seawall surface are recorded as follows: Chenhua Beach section, 140+ zhang damaged, more than 3 zhang breach; Gu Longdun section, 200+ zhang damaged, 20+ zhang breach; Zhangjiazhai section, 200+ zhang damaged, 30+ zhang collapse; Xuejiatan section, 200+ zhang damaged, 30+ zhang breach; Niutoujing section, 80+ zhang damaged, 10+ zhang breach; Beishidong section, 80+ zhang damaged; Wuyuedun section, 150+ zhang damaged, 10+ zhang breach. The above dangerous sections total more than 1,000 zhang. The narrowest part of the seawall surface is only 3-4 chi. All the breaches are temporarily blocked with old stones. Thousands of wooden piles are broken, and countless soil and stones have collapsed. Other sections are also damaged, totaling thousands of zhang, but no danger has yet occurred.

Parking Lots to be Built on Prosperous Roads in the French Concession 166

Pay a Small Fee Each Month

Someone to Take Care of It For You

The "China Press" reports that the French Concession Vehicle Department, in view of the increasing number of cars in this port and the rapid development of street traffic into a serious problem, has recently paid close attention to the management of cars and the improvement of street traffic. According to the registration of cars in the French Concession Public Works Department, there were only 95 freight cars and 1,591 passenger cars in 1925. This year, the number of freight cars has reached 1,965, and the number of passenger cars has reached 3,991, which shows the rapid increase in the number of cars in this port in recent years. As a result, the number of traffic accidents in the streets has also increased year by year. The reason for the accidents is mostly due to the overloading of freight cars and the parking of cars on narrow streets. Therefore, the department recently ordered that vehicles are not allowed to park on the southern end of Avenue Joffre and Route de Cercle, etc. The results have been quite good since the implementation. However, the lively roads such as Avenue Edward VII and Rue Cardinal Mercier lack places to park vehicles, and cars are also very inconvenient. Therefore, the department is now planning to build several parking places. Car owners can park their cars there for a small monthly fee. Someone will take care of it and provide the convenience of supplying gasoline. In addition, it is also planned to formulate special regulations that all car drivers and car owners who drive themselves must have their eyesight and hearing tested to determine whether they are suitable for driving.

The Head of the Xinmin Township in Pudong Kills a Man 167

Private Torture Leads to Serious Injury and Death

How Can Public Officials Do Such a Thing?

Zhang Chaosheng, a 37-year-old resident of Jie Gou Township near Yangjia Town in Pudong, relied on farming and fishing for a living. His wife, Zhu, gave birth to a daughter who is now 13 years old. On the night of August 6, Fan Hongsheng and Fan Quansheng invited Zhang to fish in the south bank of the Weijia Sacred Church in the east of the town. Zhang and his friend Ke Miaofa happily agreed to go. At two or three o'clock in the morning, the Fans finished fishing and left first. Zhang and Ke were still reluctant to leave. Not long after, Chen Atu, the owner of the fish pond, gathered a crowd and rushed over, tied up Zhang and Ke with ropes, and sent them to the Xinmin Township Office in the town. Yang Tingdong, the head of the township, learned the situation and ordered Zhang and Ke to be hanged on the two sycamore trees in front of the township office and beaten severely to make an example for those who stole fish. It was not until 7 a.m. that they were persuaded by others to let them down. Zhang suffered more serious injuries and was bedridden after returning home. On August 19, his wife, Zhu, saw that her husband's injuries were getting worse and his life was in danger, so she hired someone to carry Zhang to the township office to cry and make a scene. Yang, the head of the township, had no choice but to give Zhu five yuan in silver and five dou of white rice, persuading her to carry her husband home for treatment. At 1 p.m. on the 23rd, Zhang died of his injuries. Zhang's wife then went to Yang's house and cried on the ground, claiming that he should return her husband's life. Yang had no choice but to go to the Seventh District Office of Nanhui County with Zhang's wife on the 25th to discuss the funeral arrangements. Yang was willing to pay 50 yuan for coffin and funeral expenses. Zhang's wife said that after her husband's death, his wife and daughter were left behind and their livelihood was cut off. Yang should pay the mother and daughter some living expenses. The differences between the two sides were too great to be resolved. The district chief Yu Feng reported it to the Nanhui County Government. The county government appointed clerk Wang Zhongqiu and bailiff Sheng Yi to go to the countryside to inspect the body. After the inspection, they wrote an edict: "Now, Zhang Chaosheng of Jie Gou Township, 37 years old, has a fatal wound on his left rib. It is indeed that he was injured and died before his death. The body has been delayed for many days and the whole body has rotted. The wife is ordered to collect the body as soon as possible for verification." For the sake of caution, Zhang's wife entrusted Shanghai doctor Wang Jianrong to re-examine the body, and the results were as follows: (omitted above) The front end of the left rib is broken at the junction with the costal cartilage. The surrounding area is now grayish-white, and its boundary is about 2.5 inches wide and 3 inches long. It is not rotten, and there are more than a dozen small cyan dots in between. It is indeed that he was injured and died before his death. (omitted below) Since the case occurred, it has been a sensation in the surrounding villages for several days. By the time of the autopsy, the number of onlookers reached hundreds. Zhang's wife has already filed a complaint with the Nanhui County Government, accusing the township head Yang Tingdong of being a public official who privately tortured innocent people, resulting in injury and death, and requesting that he be severely punished.

Tragic Abortion 168

The Fetus is Gone but the Person Dies Tragically

Yuan, a 33-year-old woman from Yangzhou who lives at No. 1211 Wuzhou Road, had an affair with a man named Da Yanzi, a fellow villager, and became pregnant. She was about several months pregnant, and her abdomen was swollen. Feeling that it was inappropriate, she entrusted Jiangbei woman Gao Dai to introduce her to Wang Chen, a woman from the same hometown who lived at No. 69 Xinjiang Road in Zhabei Huajie, to have an abortion at about 6 p.m. on the 18th of last month. The method of abortion was to insert a medicinal herb into the lower part. After several hours, Yuan was in extreme pain and fainted, losing consciousness. Gao Dai and Wang Chen used massage to move around Yuan's abdomen. Although the fetus was gone, Yuan suffered severe injuries. She was taken to Tongren Hospital by ambulance for treatment. She died on the evening of the day before yesterday. The body was sent to the Forensic Examination Office on Feilun Road for examination. Later, the Harbin Police learned of this and ordered Detective Ruan Taibin to arrest Gao Dai and Wang Chen one after another and bring them to the police station. The police chief ordered them to be temporarily detained in the women's prison. This morning, they were escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special Court. Zhang Tianyin, the police lawyer, stated the case and said that the deceased only had a foster daughter, Zuo Dizi, 11 years old, and two landlords who lived with her. Then Qu Changfu testified that the deceased moved in last August and did not know her background, but the reason for her death was abortion. Then the girl Zuo Dizi said that the deceased called her mother. At that time, she saw the defendants rubbing her mother's abdomen vigorously with their hands. She did not know the rest. Gao Dai confessed that she was entrusted by the deceased to introduce her, and that the price was three yuan, which Wang Chen got. The rest of the confession was evasive. Wang Chen confessed that she had performed an abortion on Yuan and said that the abortion herb, named Lidan Herb, was bought from a certain drugstore. Yuan did not die on the spot, so she asked for a judgment. Judge Xiao Xiechou verified the confession and ordered the two to be detained for further interrogation at a later date.

Bandit Zhang Xiaodi Executed Yesterday by Firing Squad 169

The Shanghai-Songhu Garrison Command announced Order No. 64 of the Law:

For the purpose of announcement, according to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau's submission of a bandit named Zhang Xiaodi to the department, the investigation has been completed. Verdict in the Sino-Foreign Pharmacy Case 171

The remaining Su, Wang, and Sun were each sentenced to two years in prison and fined 4,000 yuan.

Shareholders of China Bank Sue for Illegal Election Fraud 172

The Plaintiff's Claim is Rejected

The shareholders of the China Commercial Savings Bank, Xu Yasheng, Yuan Jieqing, Wang Meizhen, Chen Anlai, etc., previously hired lawyers to sue the chairman of the bank, Guo Zhuqiao, for illegal election fraud in the Civil Court of the First Special Court. The entire board of directors of the bank, Wang Yiting, Gu Xinyi, Zhu Zikui, Zhu Ziqian, Yao Dexin, etc., believed that the plaintiff's accusations involved the board of directors, so they also hired lawyers Li Jinfu and Xu Zuyan to apply for joint participation. After Judge Shouyi's repeated interrogations, the main text of the judgment rejected the plaintiff's claim, and the litigation costs were borne by the plaintiff. The reason for the judgment was that the reason for the plaintiff's claim was whether it was reasonable or not, and whether they had the qualifications of the parties was a prerequisite issue. The total shares of China Bank are 12,500 shares, and the plaintiffs have 62 shares. This is an undisputed fact between the two parties. The dispute is whether the plaintiffs have the right to sue and whether the election by the defendants should be revoked. According to the plaintiffs' lawsuit, it is based on Article 150 of the Company Law, but the Judicial Yuan has interpreted that the so-called violations of laws and regulations only refer to the convening procedures and resolution methods. If the shareholder meeting election is fraudulent, it is not subject to the restrictions of the period of the article. Therefore, its interpretation of election fraud is not subject to the restrictions of the period of Article 150 of the Company Law, because the election fraud is different from the circumstances of the convening and resolution of the shareholder meeting violating laws and regulations, so it does not have to be restricted by the period of the article. It cannot be said that its interpretation only solves the point of the period. The plaintiffs' lawsuit against the defendant's election fraud cannot be based on the article. Article 164 of the Company Law also states that when the shareholder meeting resolves to accuse the directors or even rejects the accusation, and shareholders with more than one-tenth of the total shares apply to the supervisors, the company shall file the accusation within one month from the date of the resolution or application. Therefore, those who can file an accusation against the directors according to the article are limited to the company, and the company must also file the accusation after the shareholder meeting has resolved or shareholders with more than one-tenth of the total shares have applied to the supervisors. Now, the plaintiffs only have 62 shares and have filed a lawsuit directly with the court, which is also inconsistent with the article. The defendant's defense that they have no qualification to sue as parties has to be considered reasonable. Therefore, whether the defendant's election is illegal is not necessary to investigate. According to the above discussion, the plaintiff's claim in this case is unreasonable, and according to Article 97 of the Civil Procedure Law, a judgment is made as in the main text.

Liang Chengyu Imprisoned for Ten Years 173

Liang Declares He Must Appeal

Liang Chengyu, a Chinese detective of the Second Division of the General Inspectorate of the General Police Department, was arrested for leading a gang with weapons on April 28th of this year, at approximately 11:00 PM, and breaking into Fang Liansheng's house at No. 439 Maleli Road, Chongqing Road, and robbing morphine valued at 50,000 yuan. After the case was uncovered and he was arrested, he was sent to the First Special Court, which acquitted Liang after trial. The Police Department, dissatisfied with the verdict, filed an appeal with the Higher Court through lawyer Ru Bao-yi. After two hearings, the arguments were concluded. Yesterday morning, the date for the verdict arrived. The appellant's lawyer from the Police Department, Ru Bao-yi, and the appellee Liang Chengyu's agents, lawyers Ye Fukan and Yuan Yang'an, were all present on time. President Song Yuan, along with judges Du and Ye, took the bench and announced the verdict. The main text stated: "The original judgment is revoked; Liang Chengyu is to serve a ten-year prison sentence, with two days of detention counting as one day of imprisonment." Liang still expressed dissatisfaction after the pronouncement and declared that he must file an appeal. The President of the court granted his request.

Pudong Electric Company Collecting Additional Share Payments 175

Collection Starts Today via the Shanghai Bank

The Pudong Electric Company has been actively engaged in construction recently, sparing no effort. In May, it extended its lines to Zhangjialou, and in June, it expanded eastward to Jinjiaxiang. Starting from Zhoujiadu, it has set up feeder lines along the newly built Pudong Trunk Road of the Municipal Government, extending north to near Yangjing Port. According to the original plan, it needs to be further extended to Donggou, which should be completed in approximately November. The entire line is 20 kilometers long and can transmit 2,000 kilowatts of electricity. In other areas, new poles and lines are being installed for new users. The capacity of transformers has also increased significantly. After the completion of the Pudong Trunk Road mainline, it plans to expand from Donggou to Gaoxing Town and from Yangsi to Sanlin Town. There is also Yangjing Road, a vital thoroughfare from Lujiadu to Yangjing Town, where high-voltage lines are planned for connection. The company's total capital was originally set at 500,000 yuan, of which 400,000 yuan has already been collected, leaving 100,000 yuan uncollected. Now, due to vigorous construction and high demand for funds, the Board of Directors has decided to collect the remaining 100,000 yuan in full within two months, from September 1st to October 31st. The Shanghai Bank has been entrusted to collect the payments. It is reported that the additional share certificates have been prepared and sent to each shareholder for timely payment.

The bullets are arranged in rows of three and are not damaged. Wang Zhongli, the owner of Yufengtai Shop, and Lu Renlin, the owner of Zhonghua Copper Factory, who purchased the cartridge cases and bullets from Yufengtai, and Jin Ruitang of Yongfengyu Socks Shop, and the shop partner Fang Genji, were arrested. While the goods were being transported, they were discovered and detained by patrol officer Xu Tongchang. According to Wang Zhongli, they were purchased from the Yangzhou Road Special Patrol House. Zhang Weicheng Reports on the Recent Situation in Xiancheng 185

Japanese Spread Rumors and Anti-Chinese Sentiment Intensifies

Nearly Half of Overseas Chinese Are Returning Home

Zhang Weicheng, the consul stationed in Korea, sent a letter to Wang Xiaolai, the chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday, reporting on the Xian incident and the receipt of funds to aid overseas Chinese, saying, "In Shanghai, I had the pleasure of conversing with you. After our farewell, I returned to my post at the end of June. On July 3rd, there were anti-Chinese news reports, and I immediately warned the Governor-General of Korea and requested serious precautions and effective protection. On one hand, I sent a telegram to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the embassy in Japan (because the Governor-General and the Supervisor-General were both in Tokyo), and on the other hand, I informed all consulates in Korea. The riots there were not yet severe. From the 3rd to the 9th, I went to the Korean Governor-General's office for serious negotiations. The consulate accommodated 4,000 refugees, not including the branch consulates. My colleagues worked through the night, still worrying about the backlog. The busyness of the affairs can be imagined. Unexpectedly, riots broke out in various places, and overseas Chinese suffered greatly. The Chinese merchants in Pyongyang were almost completely wiped out and have not yet recovered. The aftermath is extremely complicated. Although the Japanese side has apologized and various places have gradually calmed down, the resentment remains deep, and the overseas Chinese are anxious. Recently, Japanese newspapers issued special editions for the Qingdao National Essence Society incident, falsely claiming that sixty Japanese were killed and twenty were injured, causing anti-Chinese sentiment to intensify again. Our consulate received warning letters from Japanese people attacking the consulate and forming suicide squads. Nearly half of the overseas Chinese are returning home. I have been ill for a month, spending my days with a medicine stove, but with many affairs and few people, I have to work hard despite my illness. It has been almost two months since the riots, and my colleagues work as usual every week without rest. In addition, there are many overseas Chinese groups with different opinions. Inwardly and outwardly, the pain is difficult to express. Knowing that you are concerned, I am only briefly reporting. I recently heard that your Municipal Chamber of Commerce has remitted nearly 7,000 yuan to the Capital Chamber of Commerce, for which I am especially grateful. I hope you will inform the donating organizations. In addition, the Korean Chinese Chambers of Commerce include more than ten locations such as Gyeongseong, Incheon, Pyongyang, Jinnampo, Busan, Sinuiju, Wonsan, Chongjin, Daegu, Unsan, Bukchin, Hamheung, and Ungcheon Seongjin, each with its own area, and there is no organization for joint meetings. There are even more chambers of commerce and public associations in small places in the outer provinces. Because overseas Chinese used to live together with Japanese and Koreans, even in remote villages there are several or dozens of Chinese families. The situation is different from elsewhere, and the affairs of the consulate are also more difficult to handle. Please pay attention."

Mining Tin Ore in He County, Guangxi

The first prize is 200 yuan in cash, the second prize is two prizes of 50 yuan each, the third prize is ten prizes of 10 yuan each, and the fourth prize is twenty prizes of 5 yuan each. However, those guessing must use ink to write the guessed number on the back of the candy wrapper, and state their name and address to be valid. The box will be opened and counted in public on September 16th, and the results will be announced in the newspaper.

Dr. Yang Zhongfu Hired to Go to Hangzhou 193

Dr. Yang Zhongfu has been practicing medicine in this port for many years, with rich experience and extremely busy practice. Now, he has been hired by two major philanthropists in Shanghai, Zhang Xiaolin and Du Yuesheng, to go to Hangzhou to establish and manage the Hangzhou Epidemic Hospital as director. He could not decline the offer. Therefore, all of Dr. Yang's medical practice in Shanghai has been stopped as of today, to avoid patients traveling back and forth.

Shanghai Correspondence Agency to Begin Publishing Today 194

The Shanghai Correspondence Agency, located at No. 7 Qunyi Lane, Ningbo Road, Public Concession, is a news organization jointly organized by industry, commerce, and academia. It has hired Zhu Yingpeng, a well-known figure in the news industry, as the president to preside over the agency's affairs. It has been decided to begin publishing today (September 1st).

Japan Research Society Gifts Issue on the Wanbaoshan Incident 195

The Japan Research Monthly, published by the Japan Research Society, is the earliest periodical in the country to study Japanese issues. Since the Wanbaoshan incident occurred, the society, in order to awaken the public's attention, has made sacrifices and specially advertised unconditional free distribution to all sectors. A total of over 20,000 requests were received. The first issue of this special edition is already published, totaling 100,000 words. The second volume of the special edition is currently in printing, with even more detailed content. Those wishing to request a copy can write to the society at No. 6 Difeng Lane, Difeng Road, without having to include postage stamps.

Echen Correspondence Agency Moves 196

The Shanghai Echen Correspondence Agency, established for three and a half years, has moved from Shangren Lane, Shandong Road, to No. 499 Xinyi Lane, Meibige Road, as of September 1st. It will continue to publish as usual. Also, the agency's telephone number has not yet been installed due to the need to change the number.

Wang Youlin Law Firm Moves 197

Lawyer Wang Youlin has been practicing law for many years. Now, due to the development of his business, the original office at No. 50 Tiantang Street, French Concession, is insufficient for use. As of September 1st, he has moved to a new building at No. 71 Xiangkang Lane, Meibige Road, British Concession.

Success of Deli Bread 198

Mr. Huang Xiqing, the owner of the Deli Bread Factory, has been doing business in Shanghai for almost twenty years, having served in various major companies with rich experience. Recognizing that bread is an increasingly needed item in society, he resigned from his company position and invited his brother Huang Jiaguang to set up a factory in Zhabei, specializing in the production of various breads, which are exceptionally beautiful, soft, fragrant, and smooth, combining all the virtues. It is deeply welcomed by society and far surpasses other types of bread. Therefore, since its opening, major companies and tea restaurants have been placing orders one after another, and demand exceeds supply.

News from Various Labor Unions 199

The Fifth District Cotton Textile Industry Labor Union held a temporary emergency meeting yesterday. Chairman Zhang Qingyun presided over the ceremony and delivered a report (omitted). Discussions included: (1) The economic hardship faced by the Rihua sub-office. The consensus was that the union should provide assistance within its means. It was resolved that, given the union's own financial difficulties, Comrade Xia Xiaomei should be asked to lend money temporarily. (2) The case of Huang Linxiang, a preparatory member of the sub-office, being suspended from work by the factory. It was resolved to conduct a detailed investigation before determining a course of action. (3) (Confidential) A portion of workers in the Fourth Department currently eat meals provided by the factory, and the factory now intends to cease providing these meals. It was resolved to demand that the factory continue providing meals as usual. The meeting was adjourned.

▲The Sixth District Enamelware Industry Labor Union held its eighth joint meeting of directors and supervisors yesterday. Chairman Zhang Chengxi began by reporting on the resolutions of the previous meeting. The meeting then commenced discussions, including: (1) The issue of holiday pay following the announcement of the Factory Act on June 1st. Despite repeated negotiations, the company has intentionally delayed. It was resolved to submit the matter to the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs for handling. (2) The conditions modified by the union following the long-ago announcement of the Factory Act have now been clearly drafted. It was proposed that these conditions be discussed item by item. A resolution was passed to adopt them and to schedule a delegates' conference to discuss them. (3) Regarding the severe flooding in sixteen provinces, how should the union express its concern? It was resolved to send a letter to the company requesting that, in accordance with the Factory Act, two days' wages from special leave be deducted and sent to the disaster relief committee within half a month for distribution to the affected areas. This was adopted. (4) How should the outstanding special donations from March be handled? It was resolved: A. Continue collecting the donations. B. Publicize the use of the collected funds through a mimeographed notice. This was adopted. (5) Confidential. (6) The company's exclusive control over the management of the business fund and the personnel responsible for it is deemed inappropriate. How should this be handled? It was resolved to send a letter to the company to express disapproval and to submit a request to the Bureau of Social Affairs for correction. This was adopted. The rest is omitted. The meeting was adjourned.

▲The Hotel and Reception Industry Labor Union held its eighth joint meeting of directors and supervisors yesterday. Chairman Zhang Yukun presided over the discussion of the following items: (1) Luo Zongshan, former standing committee member of the Beiyang Labor Union, submitted a request for prompt repayment of back wages due to financial hardship. It was resolved to send a letter to the Beiyang Office to handle the matter. (2) Directors Xu Liangyuan and Dong Shoufu submitted letters requesting permission to resign due to old age and inability to manage union affairs. It was resolved to retain them. (3) A motion to hire lawyer Mao Yun as the union's permanent legal advisor was passed. The lawyer's fees will be covered by a special donation of ten yuan from each sub-office. (4) A joint order from the Municipal Public Security Bureau and the Bureau of Social Affairs requires the union to be responsible for surrendering licenses and badges when hotels close or receptionists resign, in order to prevent abuse. It was resolved to notify all hotels to comply. (5) The South Station Outer River Sub-Office reported that when a Qingyuan ship arrived, porters robbed passengers of luggage entrusted to the receptionists for handling. It was resolved to reserve this item. (6) The Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs approved the signing of an agreement by the Sixth Sub-Office. It was resolved to instruct the executive secretaries of each office to come to the union to collect the agreement after it is approved by the Municipal Party Headquarters. (7) To avoid suspicion, the financial records should be compiled into a list for public disclosure. It was resolved that the general affairs section would be responsible. (8) The North Station Office has been established and has elected officers, submitting a request for registration. It was resolved to approve the registration and issue an official seal. (9) Membership admissions and withdrawals must be reported to the union and forwarded to higher authorities for registration. This was adopted. (10) Should the regulations for managing hotel receptionists in the city apply to receptionists on ships, requiring them to register and obtain licenses and badges from the competent authorities? It was resolved to submit a request to the Bureau of Social Affairs for guidance. (11) The accounting books of each sub-office should be unified according to accounting formats. It was resolved to adopt this.

Weather Report 200

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the coastal areas and the Yangtze River basin would be mostly cloudy. There would be southeast winds over the Yellow Sea and the East China Sea. A hurricane southeast of Luzon is clearly moving towards the Balingtang Strait. Southern Taiwan is experiencing severe weather. Also, in the 24 hours preceding 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in the city was 86.2 degrees and the lowest was 69.3 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 89.8 degrees and the lowest was 72.5 degrees.

Shen Bao Reader Communication Guidelines

The staff of this newspaper firmly believes that each of our readers has certain personal issues that urgently need discussion. Based on our spirit of service to society, we are willing to act as consultants, offering our most sincere opinions for textual deliberation. If readers can thereby obtain appropriate solutions, reduce difficulties, and increase happiness, how delightful would that be?

For the time being, the issues that readers wish to discuss with the staff of this newspaper are limited to the three categories of education, career, and marriage.

When communicating, please clearly state your surname, given name, gender, age, occupation (or school, grade), native place, and mailing address. (It is advisable to provide these details again in subsequent communications, in case the previous letter did not reach us.) Then, on a new line, clearly state the issue you wish to discuss. The writing should be detailed, accurate, and easy to understand. Please write "Shen Bao Reader Communication Department" on the envelope. Please attach sufficient postage for a reply.

When communicating, please cut out the imprint of this publication and paste it to the upper left corner of the stationery to serve as proof of correspondence.

The method of handling letters received by this newspaper: A. We will respect the reader's wishes. Any letter stating a desire not to have the reply published in the newspaper or a desire not to have their name disclosed in the reply will be respected.

B. If the letter does not specify how the reply should be handled, but the staff believes that the reply to one person has value as a reference for everyone, it will be disclosed in the newspaper.

C. If the letter states a desire for the reply to be published in the newspaper, but is limited by space, we can only disclose the essential points, or may not be able to disclose it at all, or may have to delay disclosure because the issue requires further consideration. We ask for your understanding. However, if we cannot reply in the newspaper, we will still reply by mail.

Book and Newspaper Reviews

Textile Annual (Continued) 201

— Shu Yuan

Mr. Zhu also has an article, "An Investigative Record of the Japanese Textile Industry," which is an even more valuable piece of writing. The investigation took more than a month of time, and the places visited included Japan's six major cities: Tokyo, Osaka, Yokohama, Kobe, Kyoto, and Nagasaki. According to Mr. Zhu's report, a certain textile factory in Tokyo has 120,000 spindles and 1,700 looms, producing yarn ranging from 30 counts to 120 counts, using American cotton, Sea Island cotton, and Egyptian cotton as raw materials. The factory has a total of 2,200 female workers and 500 male workers. The female workers are all young women aged 16 to 20. Board and lodging are provided by the factory, with a deduction of only 12 cents per person per day for meals. Eighteen people live in each room, and each room has a low table with books and vases for the female workers to read and use. There is a well-equipped library for female workers and two complete hospitals. Each patient has a scroll in hand. It is learned that all female workers must study for at least six years before entering the factory, so there are no illiterate workers in the factory. The factory also has classrooms and recreational facilities, and all the necessary equipment for daily life is complete. After reading the above passage, let us compare it with our country's factories. How different are they? Mr. Zhu also visited the Textile Department of Tokyo Institute of Technology, the Industrial Experiment Institute, the Umeda Steel Works, the Toyota Automatic Loom Company, the Kikuichi Textile Company, the Kishiwada Textile Company, the Uchiumi Textile Company, and other major factories, examining in detail the equipment, working conditions, types of machinery, engineering sequence, and production ratios. He also listed 30 superior points of Japanese factories for us to adopt.

Mr. Shen Panyuan's "Horsepower of Textile Machines" compares and clarifies the horsepower of cotton openers, roving frames, coarse yarn frames, and fine yarn frames, so that those who aspire to this industry have something to choose from.

Mr. Zhu Xianfang's "Overview of the Establishment and Reorganization of the Shenxin Textile Factory No. 7" describes the factory's history, the obstacles at the beginning, and the overview of the reorganization in an orderly manner. Although the equipment inside is not even one-tenth of that of Japanese factories, the planned design and step-by-step implementation will make it easy to gradually improve. Therefore, this article is of great practical reference value.

Mr. Chen Shouyi's "Installation Method of Platt Spinning Machines" explains the matters to be noted when receiving machine boxes, the matters to be noted when unpacking and cleaning machine parts, and the sequence and precautions for installing each machine, one by one. Only those who are familiar with specialized academic knowledge can write a single word.

Mr. Chen also has an article, "Belt Knowledge," which explains in detail the quality, use, design of belts with numbers and drawings. The mechanical algorithm and maintenance method of belts are also answered in depth and clearly based on scientific principles.

Mr. Cai Zhulan's "Research on Belts" First, the raw materials used for belts are described, the second section describes the belt speed, the third section describes belt transmission, the fourth section describes belt strength, the fifth section describes the horsepower required for belts, the sixth section describes belt transmission methods, the seventh section describes the length of belts, the eighth section describes belt joint methods, the ninth section describes belt protection, the tenth section describes belt selection, and the eleventh section describes belt calculation principles. Each section uses geometric formulas to explain, which is tens of thousands of words and the essence of scientific writing.

Mr. Mu Yidao's "Research on Lighting in Textile Factories" and "Research on Adjusting Humidity and Moisture in Textile Factories" are both practical studies on the equipment of textile factories, mostly from experience. However, his discussion of lighting is also in line with science and is suitable for the hygiene of workers. The research on air is translated from the original work of Tan Baisun in the United States, and the translation is fluent and readable.

Mr. Huang Yunkui's "Design of Cloth Factories" includes the description of machines, the allocation of the number of machines, the construction of factories, the arrangement of machines, the adjustment of temperature and humidity, and the installation of electric lights, and all the designs that cloth factories should have are complete with an attached diagram, which is even clearer.

In the investigation column, Mr. Ye Liang's "A Glimpse of Imported Textiles" statistically shows the import quantities of cotton yarn, wool yarn, rayon, cotton cloth, woolen fabrics, silk fabrics, and other groceries over the years, which is enough to alert people.

Guidelines for Book and Newspaper Review Manuscripts 202

(1) The writing is limited to introducing the latest publications at home and abroad. In addition to literary works, all political, economic, legal, and scientific works.

(2) Books and newspapers on education are all included in the review, but not boring legal reports.

Youth Garden

Heat 203

Hearing people say that the weather is hot, I raised my head and looked at the ceiling, and many useless things came to my mind, like I wanted to cry. I feel that those who have time to say it is hot are ultimately happy.

I remember there was a time when I couldn't settle for my quiet life and said I wanted to move, saying that young people are bravely demanding stimulation after extreme depression, so like a dream, I ran from Beiping to Nanjing to become a soldier.

Everyone was young, with fiery enthusiasm. The aspiration in front of us was revolution. The team made you dare not relax your caution from morning to night. Everyone's work was tense. Hearing the cicadas chirping in the trees, I didn't care that summer had already come. What I held in my hand was a Type 79 rifle. On the drill field, no one paid attention to the sun.

Now the environment has brought me to another world. Although I feel the pain of poverty more acutely because of illness, I have the right to sit here and write articles very peacefully. I write from morning to night, writing what to get published there. I don't even have the courage to answer myself. It seems that I understand that since society doesn't need me, I can't despise fulfilling this boring obligation.

Do they say I am a person who studies literature? I am sad. For the sake of creation, I say, try all kinds of lives. So I was like a frightened sheep, running around aimlessly. Where is the battlefield of life? When news of the war came, whether it was a victory or a defeat, I was not happy or sad. This tree, six years have passed. Looking at my thin and weak physique, touching the scars on each part, I escaped, a defeated soldier.

But I should still celebrate that I was lucky enough not to die. If I died, then the opportunity for others to laugh at my stupid behavior would also be lost. Those people, they say,

(What is life? Take a look. We are everyone's standard.)

What kind of standard is it? What I know is that they told me,

Friends, these days are too pitiful. People are so poor. Can we, knowledgeable young people, not help them get rid of it? On the one hand, we must demonstrate against the oppressors. Our responsibility is to let the forces that destroy those people be destroyed.

I dare not say whether this is right or wrong. But they say I am outdated. After a few days, they caught me again and said,

(No wonder ×× said there was no way. It's true. No one in society understands our actions. Is our time and energy only to get this bit of ridicule in return?)

Not long after these words were spoken, I met them again in the park. The time was autumn, and the wind brought a desolate feeling. The shaking shadows, I clearly knew that they were feeling confused inside.

(, Lao Wang, long time no see. Do you often come to the park to play?)

(I don't come often, because I feel that time is too tight.)

(Ah, you are really brave, someone who can say that time is too tight must have a lot of work. We always have to come here to relax every day.)

I could only smile at them. There were no appropriate words that I could use to answer that fit the current situation.

(But is there really no way out for us? The world is so big.)

(Living like this is really dangerous.)

(……)

They said several more words. I knew that if I didn't sympathize with them, they would easily laugh at me for not having suffered any setbacks.

Autumn died, and spring had already come to the world, but I never saw these people again. I knew that some people would commit suicide when they were frustrated, so I was a little worried about them. I searched for their news everywhere, but I received their replies like this,

(Friends, I'm really sorry, I ran to this very remote foreign land, and I feel it is disrespectful to write to friends in a hurry. Moreover, the life of the army makes my shadow as small as a free-floating firefly. Forgive me for not being able to write a long letter when I am too busy to shout to kill the enemy.)

Another person's letter

(...I heard that ×× is a quartermaster in the ×× army, and because he ate too much privately, he was dismissed. Did you know? It is said that dismissal is still considered a fluke... )

Some of them became teachers. Hearing others say that this friend's current argument is,

(Only by starting with education is there a good way out for young people. China is currently lacking leadership talents, and being a teacher is the first step in leadership work.)

After hearing these words, it seemed that I had forgotten the trend of this friend instigating the replacement of teachers in schools a year ago, as well as what he said at that time that education was like a blind man riding a blind horse.

Two months ago, ××, who told me that he would vow to remain single, took his lover to Open air for swimming that day. I said,

(×× Women are poisonous snakes, you said.)

×× didn't reply at the time, but a few days later, someone told me that ×× was dissatisfied with what I said to him in the swimming pool, saying that I had intentionally insulted him, and also cursed me for being corrupt and despising women's rights.

……

Thinking about it, I have been ridiculed everywhere for a long time, just like today. But can I worry about these things? Young people are all moving forward and developing in this way, but I am still sitting here, doing something close to foolish writing. What use am I?

I didn't tell anyone that my mother has been starving for a long time thousands of miles away. In the crowds on Fourth Horse Road, I found that every prostitute might be like my homeless sister. I am walking to the end of my youth. Can I say that I have been separated from happiness for a long time? ...

I feel that thinking about my own affairs is a luxury.

Hot? I will honestly do my duty with the will of the times. I want to write, and I have my actions before and after writing.

Youth Garden Manuscript Guidelines 204

(1) The writing is limited to discussions about youth issues, news and essays from schools and students at home and abroad, descriptions of school life, and handwriting as a range, regardless of style.

(2) Books are limited to those about youth issues.

(3) Photos that qualify are those of youth life (such as sports, travel, excursions, theatrical performances, lectures, gatherings, exhibitions, various competitions, etc.), school news, and youth movements. Whether individual or group, both are welcome. Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.
